 Along with fog, it is also freezing in Delhi and northern India

 pareshaani or badhane vaali he

 2019 First Lunar Eclipse Or Chandra Grahan Date, Time And Cautions: saal 2019 kaa sabase pehla chandra grahan 21 janvari yani aaj lag rahaa he
 This year, there will be an eclipse on the moon twice
 inamen sabase pehla chandra grahan aaj lag rahaa he
 After this, the second and last lunar eclipse of this year will take place on 16 July 2019
 aaj lag rahe grahan kii kul avadhi 3 ghante 30 minute kii hogi
 It is a full lunar eclipse
 yah chandra grahan kark raashi or pushya nakshatra main laga he
 This eclipse will not be seen in India
 balki, yah grahan dakshin america, europe, africa or madhya mahaasaagar main dikhaai degaa
 But this eclipse will affect everyone
 dharmik manyata or jyotishiya main chandra grahan ke dauraan kuch kaaryon ke karne ko varjit mana jaataa he
 Super Lunar Eclipse Time - 21 January Monday Eclipse Start - 9 4
45 am
 grahan madhya- param grass- subah 10 bajkar 42 minute
 Eclipse touch ends - 11 in the morning 13 minutes
 grahan samaapt- dopaher 12 bajkar 21 minute
 Let us know what things should not be done during lunar eclipse -1
 grahan ke dauraan dev puja ko nishiddh mana jaataa he
 This is the reason that the doors of temples are closed when an eclipse occurs
 2
 No auspicious work should be done during lunar eclipse
 3
 Nature becomes more sensitive during lunar eclipse
 yahi kaaran he ki is dauraan ped, paudhon or patton ko todna nahin chahie
 4
 jyotishiya dharna ke mutabik, chandra grahan ke dauraan nakhun or bal kaatane ko ashubh mana jaataa he
 5
 chandra grahan ke dauraan khaanaa banane or khaane se bachanaa chahie
 6
